 185 std::visit([i, &slice, &ret, &dimsToDrop](auto&& arg) {
278 using argT = std::decay_t<decltype(arg)>;
279 if constexpr (std::is_same_v<argT, SliceIndex>)
280 {
281 ret.m_shape[i] = 1;
282 ret.m_offset += arg.index * ret.m_strides[i];
283 dimsToDrop.emplace_back(i);
284 }
285 else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<argT, SliceRange>)
286 {
287 if (!arg.start)
288 {
289 arg.start = 0_z;
290 }
291 if (!arg.stop)
292 {
293 arg.stop = static_cast<ptrdiff_t>(ret.m_shape[i]);
294 }
295 if (!arg.step)
296 {
297 arg.step = 1_z;
298 }
299
300 auto start = *arg.start;
301 auto stop = *arg.stop;
302 auto step = *arg.step;
303
304 if (start < 0_z)
305 {
306 start = 0;
307 }
308
309 if (stop > static_cast<std::ptrdiff_t>(ret.m_shape[i]))
310 {
311 stop = ret.m_shape[i];
312 }
313
314 if (step == 0_z)
315 {
316 ret.m_shape[i] = 0;
317 }
318 else if (step > 0)
319 {
320 if (stop <= start)
321 {
322 ret.m_shape[i] = 0;
323 }
324 ret.m_shape[i] = (*arg.stop - *arg.start + *arg.step - 1_z) / *arg.step;
325 }
326 else
327 {
328 throw std::runtime_error("Negative step not supported in this release (please file an issue if you need this).");
329 }
330
331
332 ret.m_offset += *arg.start * ret.m_strides[i];
333 ret.m_strides[i] *= *arg.step;
334
335 }
336 // For SliceAll, don't modify shape
337 }, slice);
338 184 ++i;
339 }
